Exhibition Summary

Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce National Products Exhibition Conference Outline: Article 1, The conference is organized by the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, divided into two parts: display and commercial area, named the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Commodity Exhibition Hall 15th Anniversary National Products Exhibition Conference, abbreviated as Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce National Products Exhibition Conference. Article 2, The purpose of the conference is to promote the improvement of arts and crafts in various industries, expand the sales of goods, and commemorate the 15th anniversary of the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Commodity Exhibition Hall. Article 3, The display department of the conference is located on the third and fourth floors of the Commodity Exhibition Hall, and the commercial area department is located opposite the Racecourse on Jing'an Temple Road (behind Baker Road). Article 4, The conference is scheduled to open on October 1st and will last for three weeks. It may be extended if necessary. Article 5, The chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the director of the Commodity Exhibition Hall will serve as the president and vice president of the conference, respectively, in charge of all matters. Article 6, After the conference, all exhibited items will be evaluated by experts from various industries, who will form a judging committee to determine the grades and issue certificates. Article 7, All conference affairs records will be compiled and reported in a report after the conference. Article 8, This outline will be implemented after being approved by the Standing Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

Commercial Area Rules

(1) All factories wishing to participate in the commercial area of the conference must not sell non-national products or goods with altered appearances. If there is any violation, the business will be immediately suspended, and all fees paid will not be refunded and will be subject to severe penalties. (2) The locations in the commercial area are divided into three types: A, B, and C. Type A costs 50 yuan per square, Type B costs 40 yuan per square, and Type C costs 21 yuan per square. The fees must be paid in full at the time of registration. (3) The commercial area will be open from 8:30 a.m. to 8:00 p.m. daily, including Sundays. (4) Registration for the commercial area will be from now until September 25th. The registration office is located at the Commodity Exhibition Hall of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, north of Tianhou Palace Bridge. (5) Factories participating in the sale of goods must register them first. Without approval, they may not sell products from other companies to avoid disputes. (6) Each square in the commercial area will be provided with two 25-candlepower light bulbs. If additional lights are desired or the light intensity is increased, it will be calculated at value (all using domestic light bulbs). (7) The layout of each factory should be simple and beautiful, and should not be done carelessly or occupy the road. (8) Employees dispatched by each factory must wear national clothing and wear the conference badge, and must observe courtesy and obey the guidance of the conference management staff. (9) All products of each factory must be clearly marked with the actual code and must not be subject to haggling or the sale of inferior goods.

Zhejiang Local Bank Handles Agricultural Loans 87

Divided into Cooperation, Seedling, Storage and Pledge, etc.; Total Loan of 3.81 Million

Xinsheng News Agency reports that Zhejiang Local Bank, in view of the increasingly dilapidated rural economy, the depletion of agricultural resources, and the increasingly difficult livelihood of farmers, has specially set up an Agricultural and Industrial Loan Department to be responsible for handling agricultural and small-scale industrial loans. Since its establishment, it has achieved considerable results. A visit and report are as follows:

Agricultural Cooperative Loans

To help rural areas, such as by using a cooperative system to lay its foundation, there will be no worries about capital concentration, and there will be fair distribution. Its prosperity and growth can be expected while standing firm. Therefore, agricultural financial institutions have always targeted rural cooperatives to achieve twice the result with half the effort. The handling of rural cooperatives in our country dates back more than ten years. After the Northern Expedition, rural credit cooperatives in various provinces were organized one after another. However, due to the poor rural environment and the lack of knowledge among farmers in our country, there are still not many cooperatives that are well-organized and whose members understand the true meaning of cooperation. In this situation, it seems insufficient in both quantity and quality to rely solely on cooperative organizations to regulate the rural economy. From the beginning, our bank has advocated lending to cooperatives and stipulated that lending to farmers' cooperatives should be the principle of agricultural lending. However, due to the above-mentioned reasons, coupled with the fact that many cooperatives in Zhejiang Province have close relationships with local agricultural financial institutions, the promotion of cooperative loan business seems to be slightly slow. However, when cooperatives need larger loans or need funds to carry out special businesses, they often borrow from our bank. In the past year, in addition to lending to agricultural financial institutions in various places for re-lending to cooperatives, the amount of direct lending to cooperatives has reached more than 284,000 yuan.

Agricultural Seedling Loans

Seedling loans are the first step to increase farmers' production and promote agricultural improvement. They are deeply and significantly related to agriculture. When farmers are plowing and planting in the spring, they often have to make do with whatever is available due to lack of funds when it comes to the selection of seeds and fertilizers, as well as the equipment for farming tools and machinery, making it difficult to expect a good harvest. After a disastrous year, there are also many places where poverty has reached the point where they cannot even sow seeds. Under these circumstances, if there are no financial institutions that provide low-interest loans for turnover, the general farmers will inevitably still rely on the old-fashioned high-interest loans, which is like drinking poison to quench thirst, and the harm will be even deeper, which will further plunge the rural areas into a state of collapse. Our bank is keenly aware of this and has spared no effort in promoting agricultural seedling loans, conducting trials in more than ten places such as Yuqian, Ningbo, and Hangzhou counties, and the results have been quite good. Farmers have been able to use the loans for production and repay them on time without any arrears. As of the end of June this year, the total amount of loans issued for this item was more than 227,500 yuan.

Agricultural Warehouse Storage Pledge Loans

Agricultural warehouse storage pledge loans are the most important and the largest in our bank's agricultural loans. The reason is that our bank has more than 50 branches, spread across all important cities and towns in the province, most of which have warehouses, making it very convenient to handle this business. Whenever the agricultural products are harvested, the prices tend to fall. Farmers who need funds can store and pledge rice, beans, wheat, etc. to the bank. The procedures are simple and the benefits are numerous. In the past year, the total amount of loans issued was more than 3,005,000 yuan. In addition, loans are also given to agricultural warehouses run by agricultural financial institutions in various counties as working capital for storing rice and grain. Our bank can also do its part to guide and assist, and the results have been quite good.

Scattered Movable Property Pledge

In recent years, the need for financial regulation in rural areas has become extremely urgent. However, the organization of cooperatives, the target of loans, is difficult to maintain, resulting in financial institutions' efforts to promote loans to rural areas, although they have done their best, have not achieved universal success. Based on our past experience, we deeply know that farmers are quite able to abide by credit. Unless it is absolutely necessary, they will never deny or delay the debts they owe. Therefore, we cannot deny them the opportunity to obtain loans simply because they do not have a cooperative organization. The only way to remedy this is to conduct pawn-style rural scattered movable property pledge loans, in order to achieve the purpose of relief. The scope of collateral for this loan includes clothing, gold and silver, copper and iron utensils, as well as raw materials and seeds. These types of pledges are owned by most farmers. In the past, they could be pledged to pawnshops at any time for turnover. However, since the inland pawn industry has been hit by the trend in recent years, many pawnshops have been unable to maintain their operations and have closed down. Even those who can barely maintain their operations have tightened their terms (i.e., deductions from the pledged price) and closed their doors (i.e., limiting the maximum pledge price to a few yuan and the total amount of loans issued per day to a few hundred yuan), etc., which often occur during financial crunches. The impact on farmers' livelihoods is not insignificant. Therefore, at a time when rural cooperatives have not yet been universally established and the pawn industry is on its last breath, conducting pawn-style rural scattered movable property pledge loans is actually an urgent task to help farmers. In view of this, our bank conducted trials in Huzhou and Lanxi branches and Changxing office in the 23rd and 24th years of the Republic of China. Not only were the farmers satisfied, but they were also able to redeem their goods upon maturity without any loss. In January of the 25th year of the Republic of China, our bank added a Longxi office, and its main task was almost entirely to operate this business. As for Fenghua, Jiashan and other places, they are also surveying houses and will open for business soon. In addition, our bank charges only 1.5% per month for insurance, interest, custody and other expenses for this type of loan, which is considered to be light on the farmers' burden. The total amount of loans pledged for this item, as of the end of June this year, reached 296,000 yuan.

Joint Guarantee Credit

Our bank has always focused on universality and practical results in agricultural lending. For farmers who are diligent, simple, poor, and have not yet joined cooperatives, those who have scattered movable property that can be pledged can pledge loans in accordance with the regulations of our bank on scattered movable property pledge loans. Those who have no movable property to pledge but are honest and diligent are also given the opportunity to obtain loans to enhance their production capacity. This is the purpose of our bank's creation of joint guarantee credit loans. According to the loan method, the borrower only needs to find three guarantors recognized by our bank from among acquaintances (most of whom are farmers) to provide joint guarantee, and then they can apply for a loan. In this way, on the one hand, honest farmers can have the convenience of financial turnover, and on the other hand, they can be made to understand the meaning of joint responsibility, arouse interest in cooperation, and lay the foundation for organizing cooperatives in the future. Currently, trials are being conducted in Lingjiaqiao and other places in Hangzhou County, and a total of more than 5,000 yuan has been issued in loans. Although the amount is not large, the benefits received by tenant farmers are not small, and it can be said to have considerable results. It is now planned to vigorously expand it in order to promote it to other places. The total amount of the above-mentioned rural loans reaches more than 3,818,000 yuan. The geographical distribution covers all important cities and towns in the province. Although the loan methods are different, their purpose of benefiting rural areas is the same.

County Government Prepares to Levy Land Value Tax 89

Provisional Measures for Collection Passed Yesterday

The Shanghai County Government, upon order, conducted a pilot land value tax. The Director of the Land Administration Bureau was previously ordered to prepare various procedures, which have been completed. County Magistrate Li, considering that the opening of the tax is approaching and the matter is a pioneering undertaking, all collection methods should invite county party and government agencies, as well as leaders from various districts, to discuss together in order to maximize the benefits. At 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the county government specially held a land value tax discussion meeting. Wang Chengyao, Zhang Yi, Zhu Changlin, Cao Yiguang, Ge Xiusheng, Zhang Jingye, Yin Xiongfei, Cao Yuanxun, and Secretary Wu and Section Chief He of the county government attended. The meeting was chaired by Li Zhifu (Section Chief He acted on his behalf), and Cao Yuanxun took the minutes. After the salutations, the process of being ordered to conduct a pilot land value tax was reported. Then, a draft of the provisional measures for collecting land value tax was submitted for discussion. After detailed research by the representatives in accordance with laws and regulations, the original proposal was revised and passed. The revised measures are recorded as follows: (1) The land in each district, township, and town of this county shall be subject to land value tax in accordance with the provisions of these measures, and the original agricultural tax shall be abolished. (2) The land value tax in each district, township, and town of this county shall be collected by the Land Tax Collection Office of the county government. (3) All land value tax is local tax, with 40% remitted to the province and 60% to the county. (4) The land value tax rate shall be 1% per year according to the estimated land value. (5) For wasteland in cities and towns that has been improved within the statutory time limit, if it is not implemented after the deadline, in addition to collecting taxes in accordance with the provisions of Article 4, the land value tax rate of 4/1000 may be increased from the year following the deadline. The scope of land improvement in the preceding paragraph shall be jointly drafted by the county government and the Land Administration Bureau and submitted to the provincial government for approval before implementation. (6) The collection date and procedures for land value tax shall be handled in accordance with the regulations on the collection of land tax in various counties of Jiangsu Province. (7) Those who fail to pay the land value tax overdue shall be subject to a late payment penalty of 3% in accordance with the order. If the overdue period exceeds the fiscal year, a late payment penalty of 6% shall be added. If the overdue period is three years or more, the county government may submit a request to the Finance Department and forward it to the provincial government for approval to auction the land with outstanding taxes and its fixtures. The proceeds shall be used to offset the outstanding taxes. If there is still a shortfall, the original tax debtor shall make up the difference, and any surplus shall be returned to the original tax debtor. (8) The reduction and exemption of land value tax shall be handled in accordance with the regulations on the reduction and exemption of taxes. (9) These measures shall be submitted by the Finance Department to the Provincial Government for approval and implementation. The meeting adjourned after the discussion. Another meeting will be held at 2:00 p.m. today to review the difference between the new tax and the old tax in this county and the methods to make up for it.

Tea Production Area Inspection Results Satisfactory; Qihong and Tunlv Concluded One After Another; Inspection Personnel Returned to Shanghai One After Another 90

In order to fundamentally improve the quality of Chinese tea and revitalize foreign trade, the National Product Inspection Committee of the Ministry of Industry held tea production area inspections. This year, it started with the Qihong and Tunlv areas first. Qihong has been completed, and Tunlv was also completed on the 15th of this month. The inspection personnel previously entrusted to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau to recruit have also returned to Shanghai one after another since August 3, led by Fan Hejun, a member of the Tea Production Area Inspection Committee, to practice in the tea area. According to Fan's report yesterday, the results of this trip were quite good. Fan said that after the end of the Qihong area production area inspection and returning to Shanghai, he was ordered to lead twelve inspection personnel to leave Shanghai on August 3 and rush to Qimen to practice the production of red and green tea. Those who practiced at the Qimen Tea Improvement Center spent fifteen days learning, picking leaves in the morning, explaining theory at noon, and manufacturing on site in the afternoon. They also experienced rural life in the nearby tea areas in order to truly understand the rural economic situation, living habits, and drawbacks. Looking at the situation in the Qihong and Tunlv areas as a whole, the most fundamental drawbacks that affect the future of Chinese tea are several reasons: (1) Due to the high and then low prices in Shanghai, inland tea companies have the bad habit of rushing to produce, resulting in tea farmers' sour, wet, smoky, and sun-dried embryos being rushed to be purchased by tea companies as long as they are early, while high-quality mountain goods and dry embryos are often unable to be sold at a good price because the buds are slower to sprout and they are not in time for the opening of the market. If this is not corrected, the quality of Chinese tea will never be improved. (2) Because tea companies have no fixed form, most of them are established with temporary investment, which has a speculative nature. They cannot unite to operate on a large scale, have no machinery and equipment, do not study and learn, and the cost is increasing and the quality is decreasing, causing a fatal blow to Chinese tea. (3) Due to the legacy of serfdom, it has not been completely eradicated, and the trend of high-interest debt is more serious than in other places. The organization of cooperative undertakings is also hindered by the above-mentioned class system. The above three reasons are based on the perspectives of tea merchants, tea companies, and tea farmers, and are the basic factors for the decline of the tea industry in the area. Now the central and local governments have decided to rectify the foreign trade of Chinese tea and reverse the decline. It is hoped that future facilities and plans will pay close attention to the above points, and then the future of Chinese tea may have the hope of innovation.

Citizens Have Two Special Electoral Rights; Should Choose One to Exercise; Explanation from the Electoral Office of Four Provinces 92

Guomin News Agency reports that the Shanghai National Assembly Representative Election Office received a letter from the National Assembly Representative Election Office of the Four Northeastern Provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe, Province Letter No. 98, which stated, "The case investigation shows that many citizens in the register of citizens residing in the four northeastern provinces sent by Nanjing and other places are affiliated with the military. That is, if a citizen has more than two electoral rights, which election should he participate in? There are no clear regulations in the law. May I, by analogy with the precedent of the third occupational election in Article 5 of the National Assembly Representative Election Law, order him to choose one place by himself? This office has sent a letter to the General Office of the National Assembly Representative Election for interpretation. The reply is now approved, 'The matter of those who have more than two special electoral rights is the same as those who have more than two electoral rights in occupational elections. They can naturally be handled by analogy.' I hereby reply for your information, etc. In addition to sending letters separately, I also request you to check and verify this to Jiang Zuobin, the supervisor of the Shanghai National Assembly Representative Election Office." The reporter notes that the original text of Article 5, Paragraph 3 of the Election Law is "Those who have more than two electoral rights in occupational elections shall be allowed to choose to be electors of one group." It is also reported that the oath registration of citizens in various public and private institutions in this city is still continuing. In the past few days, the Academia Sinica, the General Management Office of the Bank of China, and the Daxin Company have also held them in turn.

Ministry of Finance Approves That Silver Receipt Has Permanent Nature 93

No Formal Receipt Changed for Years

Should Be Regarded As A Formal Receipt Must Affix Stamps

The Bankers Association notified various banks regarding the issue of stamp duty on silver receipts, saying, "Dear Sirs, The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce recently requested the Ministry of Finance to exempt silver receipts issued by the silver industry from stamp duty because they were temporary in nature. The Ministry of Finance stated that many of these temporary receipts have not been exchanged for formal receipts for years and months in order to avoid tax obligations. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance approved the Chamber of Commerce's request. As a result, the Banking Association, the Stamp Duty Committee, held a meeting to study the matter. It was generally agreed that the temporary receipts commonly used by the industry are mostly for waiting for the payment to be collected or the procedures to be completed, and can be used to exchange for formal receipts or certificates. Their nature is no different from temporary subscription receipts and do not need to be stamped. This is completely different from the point mentioned by the Ministry of Finance that formal receipts have not been exchanged for years and months. If there is such a case, it should be stamped. Afterwards, each colleague should only issue temporary receipts for those who can exchange for formal receipts, certificates, or original documents in a short period of time. The said receipt must also state the words 'for the exchange of receipts, certificates, or original documents' to show the restriction. If all can be handled in accordance with this, it will not conflict with the spirit of the Ministry of Finance's approval and there is no need to affix stamps. Those that are permanent in nature and may not be exchanged for formal receipts for years and months should be regarded as formal receipts and must be stamped in accordance with the law, etc." That is, based on the said resolution, we requested the Association for review. After being submitted to the 12th Executive Committee meeting for discussion, everyone agreed with the measures proposed by the Committee. Accordingly, all banks in the Association are notified that temporary receipts issued in the future should be handled in accordance with the said measures so as not to conflict with the Ministry of Finance's approval. Please check and verify.

Social Affairs Bureau Announces Revision of Banking Regulations: Nine Chapters, Thirty Articles 97

The Shanghai Banking Association's regulations, after being revised by the Social Affairs Bureau upon request, were reported to the Municipal Government's Bureau of Industry and the Ministry of Finance. Notices were also sent to the Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and various courts. The full text of the announced regulations is as follows: Shanghai Banking Regulations, Revised June 25th. Chapter 1: General Principles. Article 1: These regulations are the common rules for the business operations of member banks of the Shanghai Banking Association, and are named the Shanghai Banking Regulations. Chapter 2: Business Hours and Holidays. Article 2: Business hours are from 9:00 AM to 4:00 PM daily. Banks that close on Saturday afternoons will close at 12:00 PM. However, banks may extend these hours according to their customs, but must report this to the association for record. The time for interbank check clearing is from 9:00 AM to 3:00 PM daily, but for banks that close on Saturday afternoons, it is until 12:00 PM. Article 3: Holidays are as follows: 1. Sundays; 2. National Day (October 10th); 3. New Year's Day (from January 1st to 4th); 4. Mid-year Settlement (July 1st and 2nd); 5. Spring Festival (one day), Summer and Autumn Festivals (one day each). (The annual holiday dates will be determined by the association at the end of each preceding year and announced.) 6. Customary holidays of Chinese and foreign banks (each bank may take holidays according to custom, but must report them to the association for record). Chapter 3: Types of Business. Article 4: 1. Various time deposit, demand deposit and savings deposits; 2. Time deposit, demand deposit, and mortgage loans; 3. Mortgage overdrafts; 4. Acceptance and discounting of drafts; 5. Domestic and foreign remittances and documentary bills; 6. Collection of funds; 7. Buying and selling bullion, foreign currencies, and securities; 8. Safekeeping of valuables; 9. Warehouse business; 10. Trust business; 11. Government-entrusted agency and franchise business. The types of business mentioned above should still be handled by each bank in accordance with its articles of association approved by the ministry. Chapter 4: Standard Currency. Article 5: All receipts and payments shall be made in national currency in accordance with the Ministry of Finance's order of November 4, 1935. Chapter 5: Interest Rates. Article 6: Interest rates for various deposits, loans, and discounts shall be determined according to the market supply and demand. Chapter 6: Important Documents. Article 7: Various deposit slips, passbooks, drafts, promissory notes, checks, and receipts issued by banks must be signed or stamped by the bank's general manager, assistant manager, deputy manager, or authorized officer. Article 8: Deposit slips, passbooks, and various receipts are not transferable. Article 9: Banks issuing term promissory notes must not exceed ten days from the date of issuance. Article 10: For current account holders who withdraw funds by check, the deposit book (i.e., receipt slip) should be stamped with the bank's receipt stamp and signed or stamped by an important officer. Chapter 7: Important Procedures. Article 11: When customers deposit funds or entrust items for safekeeping, they must leave a seal impression for verification when withdrawing in the future. If the customer requests that the bank not keep a seal impression and only withdraw funds based on the document, the bank may comply with the request, but will not be responsible for any unforeseen circumstances. Article 12: Customers who use checks to withdraw funds must leave a seal impression for the bank to pay. When opening an account, except for those familiar to the bank, a proper introduction is required. Article 13: Drafts, promissory notes, and checks are divided into registered and unregistered types. For unregistered ones, payment is made upon presentation of the document. For registered ones, payment can only be made after the payee endorses it. If the bank has doubts about the endorsement, it may require the bearer to provide sufficient proof before making payment. However, the bank is not responsible for verifying the authenticity of the endorsement or whether the bearer is the rightful owner. Article 14: Banks will not accept crossed checks for deposit unless they are from regular customers or have an introducer. Article 15: When a current account holder exchanges a check for a promissory note at the bank, the issuer must add the words "Please exchange for promissory note" on the original check and sign or stamp it with the original seal impression before it can be exchanged. Article 16: If the amount of a check issued by a depositor exceeds the deposit balance, the bearer should return the original check to the issuer for correction before payment. However, upon the bearer's request, the bank may pay part of the amount. Article 17: Certification of checks and acceptance of drafts should be indicated on the face of the document with the words "Certified" or "Accepted," along with the date, and signed or stamped by the bank's general manager, assistant manager, deputy manager, or authorized officer. Article 18: Verification of promissory notes is solely for verifying the authenticity of the document and whether there are any disputes or reported loss for stop payment. After the bank verifies that there are no errors, an important officer should sign or stamp to certify it. Article 19: For all remittances such as telegraphic transfers and mail transfers, the bank should first send the original and duplicate receipts or notify the payee to collect the funds at the bank. If the bank has doubts about the signature or seal impression on the receipt, it may require the payee to provide sufficient proof before payment. Article 20: If the bank encounters any discrepancies in the format or procedures of various negotiable instruments, or insufficient funds, it must issue a reason slip and return it to the bearer along with the instrument. Chapter 8: Reporting Loss and Stop Payment. Article 21: If various deposit slips, passbooks, and receipts are lost, the owner may submit a written application to the bank stating the reason for reporting the loss and requesting stop payment, and publish a notice in at least two reputable newspapers approved by the bank for three days to declare the document invalid. At the same time, a reliable guarantor must be invited to fill out a guarantee form. After two months, if there are no disputes, the bank can issue a new document. Article 22: Reporting the loss of a promissory note is limited to cases of fire, robbery, or loss in transit, or other matters prescribed by law. The owner of the lost document must submit a written application to the bank stating the reason for reporting the loss and requesting stop payment, and publish a notice in at least two reputable newspapers approved by the bank for three days to declare the document invalid. At the same time, a reliable guarantor must be invited to fill out a guarantee form. After two months, if there are no disputes, payment can be made. Article 23: If drafts and checks issued by the bank are lost, the owner of the lost document may request the bank to report the loss and stop payment. The procedures in Article 22, paragraph 1, apply. Article 24: If a check issued to the bank by a current account holder is lost, the issuer may apply to the bank to report the loss and stop payment. However, for checks that have already been certified by the bank, the procedures for reporting loss and stopping payment apply to Article 22, paragraph 1. If the bearer loses the check and cannot obtain the issuer's application for the time being, the bank may require them to provide a guarantee and allow temporary stop payment. Article 25: If a customer loses the seal impression used for record-keeping, the owner of the lost seal must bring the original document to the bank to report the loss. At the same time, a notice must be published in two reputable newspapers approved by the bank for three days to declare the document invalid. If there are no disputes, a reliable guarantee must be obtained to replace the seal with a new one. Article 26: The bank is not responsible if the funds have already been paid out or the entrusted items for safekeeping have already been delivered before the application for reporting loss and stop payment for various documents and seals. Article 27: If the bank believes that there are still doubts about the procedures for requesting the reporting of loss and stop payment for various documents and seals, it may require the owner of the lost document or their related parties to apply to the competent court for a public notice. Chapter 9: Supplementary Provisions. Article 28: Member banks of this association may formulate their own detailed business rules within the scope of these regulations, but must submit them to the association for record. Article 29: If there are any omissions in these regulations, or if there are any practical obstacles, this association may request revisions or be ordered to revise them directly by the Social Affairs Bureau, and report them to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance for record. Article 30: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval and promulgation by the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, and shall be reported to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance for record.

Eurasia Aviation Corporation Aviation Insurance: 10,000 Yuan Coverage per Passenger, Additional Coverage Available; Simple Procedures, Still in Initial Stages in the Country 98

According to the Central News Agency, the Eurasia Aviation Corporation is offering aviation insurance, as reported in the newspapers. Yesterday, we received a dispatch from Nanjing regarding the insurance procedures, stating that passengers must first apply for insurance, and the premium is an additional 50%. Our reporter went to the company to inquire and learned that the insurance has been implemented since the 1st, and the regulations and premiums differ greatly from the dispatch. The accurate details are recorded below:

10,000 Yuan Coverage per Passenger

The company's contract with the insurance company provides coverage of 10,000 yuan per passenger. The premium is included in the ticket price and borne by the company, so it is a passive insurance in nature. When purchasing a ticket or taking a special flight, or when the company issues an official ticket, the premium is calculated according to the mileage and sent to the insurance company. In the event of an accident, passengers can claim compensation from the company with their ticket. The company has always provided individual insurance for its flight personnel, such as pilots, mechanics, and radio operators. If they are not serving on the original aircraft, they will also be issued a ticket, and the insurance rate is up to 5% of the ticket price.

Stipulated Compensation Conditions

If passengers want to purchase additional insurance, there are also premiums for additional coverage. Calculated for every 10,000 yuan, it is 3 yuan for up to 400 kilometers, 4 yuan for 401 to 1,000 kilometers, and 6 yuan for over 1,000 kilometers. This will also be implemented soon. The compensation conditions are: (1) death due to an airplane accident; (2) total disability due to an airplane accident; (3) injury due to an airplane accident that results in complete inability to work for a short period of time, with a maximum of 10 yuan per day for recuperation expenses. When claiming compensation, in addition to the ticket or ticket stub mentioned above, a certificate from a licensed physician or a certificate from a local official must also be submitted. However, the insurance company reserves the right to appoint its own physician for re-examination. If there are doubts about the claimant's succession rights, the claimant should obtain a confirmation document from the court in accordance with non-contentious event procedures.

Extremely Cautious Handling

Since this insurance is the first time the company has handled it in China, the contact and progress have been very cautious. The aim is to simplify the procedures and keep the premiums low, with the premise of not charging passengers additional premiums. After much negotiation, an agreement was finally reached with the German Xu Qiujia Company. It is now being submitted to the Ministry of Transportation for record, and detailed regulations will be printed and distributed to various branch stations and offices for compliance. After the implementation of this type of insurance, the company's business will surely develop further.

Domestically Produced Real Silk Fabrics: Only Need Certification from Association 100

No longer need to apply to Customs for transportation and sales permits. The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Silk Weaving Joint Association is convening a second conference on the 26th to discuss methods for transporting and selling silk fabrics. Yesterday, a notice was sent to all members stating: "To our esteemed members, since the Ministry of Finance announced the methods for inspecting imported goods and requiring permits, the railway authorities have also required domestically produced real silk fabrics to have permits before being allowed to be loaded and transported. As a result, real silk goods in Shanghai have been blocked and cannot be transported. After repeated discussions and resolutions by Mr. Wang Jie'an, a standing committee member of this association, with the Nanjing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railway authorities, it has been agreed that domestically produced real silk fabrics do not need Customs transportation and sales permits. Only a certificate from the Shanghai Trade Association proving that they are domestically produced real silk fabrics is required for normal passage. We are specially informing you of this by letter, and we hope that your association will inform all fellow traders. In the future, domestically produced real silk fabrics transported by rail from Shanghai only need a certificate from the Trade Association, and it must be clearly stated that they are 'domestically produced real silk fabrics' to avoid misunderstandings by the railway authorities and detention of the goods. Foreign real silk fabrics still need to obtain Customs transportation and sales permits before they can be transported and sold. Please pay close attention. Furthermore, this association has now scheduled a conference of industry representatives from both provinces on September 26th (Saturday) at 3:00 PM at the association's location at No. 9 Gaodun Street, Shanghai, to discuss important issues. We sincerely hope that your association will send several representatives to attend and participate in the discussions and resolutions, and implement them. We eagerly await your arrival."

Mr. Tang Shaochuan officiated the wedding. After the ceremony, Mr. Tang gave a congratulatory speech, and the hosts, Mr. Yu and Mr. Zhou, gave thank you speeches. Mr. Yu also said, "My son's wedding is honored to have the respected Mr. Tang Shaochuan, who is admired throughout the country, as the officiant, and to have friends and relatives from all walks of life attend. This is a great honor. This wedding date of September 17th, although chosen by my son and daughter, happens to be the 10th anniversary of the Wuyuan Oath of the National Army. Ten years ago today, I was carrying a staff and traveling in the Mongolian desert. After traveling for dozens of days and tens of thousands of miles, I arrived at Wuyuan in hardship and difficulty, representing the Chinese Kuomintang, holding the national flag in my left hand and the party flag in my right hand, and awarding them to Mr. Feng Huanzhang, establishing the National Army in the Northwest, first relieving the siege of Shaanxi, and then joining forces in Zhengzhou. The north was pacified, and the unification of China by the Central National Revolutionary Army was achieved. Today, Mr. Feng Huanzhang is in Nanjing, holding a grand commemoration meeting, which further evokes my thoughts of today ten years ago. For the past ten years, I have only struggled for the party and done my best for the country with the spirit of hardship and difficulty. Therefore, what I hope for my son and daughter is not to inherit my property, and I have no property to give. I only hope that you can accept my decades of spirit of hardship and continue to struggle, so that you will not fail the hopes of our country for you young people, and you will be worthy of Mr. Tang and the good intentions of guests from all walks of life." Afterwards, Mayor Wu Tiecheng gave a speech on behalf of the guests. After the ceremony, the Yu and Zhou families hosted a banquet, and the toasting and conversation were very lively and grand for a time.

Wuhu Customs Commissioner's Reply to the National Private Inspection Association's Letter Regarding Extension of Registration 103

The National Private Inspection Association previously received a letter from the Wuhu County Chamber of Commerce, requesting that it forward a letter to the Wuhu Customs, allowing shops that have not yet registered to be certified by the Chamber of Commerce and complete registration. After forwarding the letter, the following reply was received from Wuhu Customs Commissioner Lordell: "I have received your association's letter of the 3rd of this month, stating that the Wuhu County Chamber of Commerce has sent a telegram requesting that a letter be forwarded to the Wuhu Customs, allowing factories and companies certified by the Chamber of Commerce to complete registration in order to provide relief. I am writing to request clarification. I have checked the recently revised types of imported goods that should be inspected, and this customs has already made a public announcement on August 31st of this year. Merchants transporting and selling newly added goods should immediately register and obtain permits in accordance with the Ministry's registration and permit issuance methods. According to the first item of the regulations, the application form should be prepared and submitted to the customs for registration and permit issuance. According to the second item of the regulations, the permit issuance period should be limited to 20 days from the date of the public announcement in the local area. However, after the deadline, new or reopened factories, companies, and transportation companies that present a valid certificate requesting registration, this customs can handle it at its discretion. The letter has been approved as requested. I am writing to reply for clarification and notification."

Macy's Report: The Aftermath of Chen's Death and Compensation 107

Chen's Wife Had a Formal Request; The Mutual Aid Society Did Not Intervene in the Compensation Amount

Regarding the case of rickshaw puller Chen Huizhang (rickshaw license no. 16863) who was beaten to death by a British sailor, and his wife's receipt of compensation from the British military authorities, there have been various and conflicting rumors circulating. The Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society specifically convened a board meeting on the 14th of this month to discuss this matter. Given the nature of the discussion, Chairman Macy specially nominated Mr. Han Yushan as temporary chairman. After this was approved, deliberations began immediately. Some argued that Chairman Macy's handling of the matter was a case of exceeding his authority. Therefore, it was decided at the board meeting on the 8th of this month to request Macy to report the details of the process. Macy then submitted the following report to the board: "In the past, when member rickshaw pullers encountered misfortunes in their daily work, the Mutual Aid Society would assist them in obtaining appropriate compensation for their losses. This is indeed a useful service that our society provides to its members. After the Chen Huizhang incident, Chen's wife immediately requested assistance from the society on July 13th. The insurance money of forty yuan was immediately paid to her. However, Chen Huizhang's death was due to a fight with a British sailor, a special circumstance. Therefore, the society's staff consulted the chairman on how to handle the issue of compensation in order to comply with the proper procedures. The chairman then advised that the matter should be closely monitored at all times, and that every effort should be made to obtain compensation from the relevant parties. In the days that followed, it was suddenly heard that an organization called the 'Support Association' had been formed, with the general aim of punishing the murderer, and with some quasi-political issues mixed in. Upon hearing this, the chairman immediately instructed the secretary-general to handle the matter cautiously. Unless Chen's wife came to the society to plead and sign a request, no action should be taken on her behalf. Subsequently, Chen's wife did come to the society to request assistance in pursuing compensation, and drafted a formal request, which is currently kept in the Shanghai Local Court. From the moment the Mutual Aid Society accepted Chen's wife's request, it instructed its staff to arrange for Chen's wife to meet with the British military representative. As a result, on July 22nd, the chairman led Chen's wife to the police station to meet Deputy Chief Inspector Yang (a British person), who was entrusted by the British military authorities to handle this matter. Mr. Xu, a staff member of the Mackenzie Road office, and another person, said to be Chen Huizhang's brother, accompanied Chen's wife. The chairman withdrew after a few minutes of introductions and did not participate in the negotiations. Afterwards, Chen's wife reported to the chairman's office that further negotiations would continue the next morning. After the second round of negotiations the next day, Chen's wife came to the society and stated that she had agreed to accept six hundred yuan as full compensation, and that she could collect the compensation that afternoon. That afternoon, Chen's wife returned to the chairman's office with the compensation of six hundred yuan. The chairman immediately advised her that such a large sum should be deposited in a bank for safekeeping, but as she did not know how to do so, she took one hundred yuan with her, and temporarily deposited five hundred yuan in the office of the Rickshaw Affairs Committee. The next day, after this sum was returned to Chen's wife, she immediately took it to the Bank of China, deposited four hundred yuan, and kept one hundred yuan for her own expenses. The foregoing is the whole story of the Mutual Aid Society's involvement in the matter. At the time, Chen's wife was extremely satisfied with the resolution and very grateful for the assistance provided by the Mutual Aid Society. However, the Mutual Aid Society never considered the political aspects of the matter or the issue of punishing the murderer, as these matters were not within the scope of the society's responsibilities." During the discussion of the aforementioned report, Macy further stated that he had never said a word about the amount of compensation. He felt that his task was completed after he introduced Chen's wife to the British military representative, and that Chen's wife was accompanied by the deceased's brother, so there was no need for him to participate in the negotiations. Some said that Macy, as a foreigner, did not value the lives of Chinese people very much. Macy said that this statement was unreasonable and he did not want to argue against it, but he felt that Chen's wife's acceptance of the compensation was the most appropriate course of action, because otherwise, it would be necessary to resort to legal proceedings, and the outcome was highly uncertain. Furthermore, the Mutual Aid Society had previously mediated hundreds of disputes, large and small. If this matter were to be handled by the relief committee or the board, on the one hand, the procedure would be too cumbersome, and on the other hand, the matter was not within the scope of relief. Chen's wife's acceptance of the six hundred yuan compensation was entirely of her own volition, and she told those she spoke to that she was satisfied with the resolution. Regarding the suggestion that such matters should be handled by the relief committee, Macy said that last year alone, a total of two thousand three hundred and thirty-six cases, large and small, were mediated. If each and every one of them had to be handled by the relief committee or the board, it would be procedurally impossible. In the end, it was decided that the board should organize a special committee in the future, so that when the staff encountered difficult problems, they could report to the committee for instructions. It was also resolved to express confidence in Mr. Macy, but this resolution should only be regarded as Mr. Macy's personal action, and not as something for which the board should be responsible. At that time, someone also mentioned the problem of the decreasing number of rickshaws. Mr. Macy (who had returned to the position of chairman) immediately stated that this matter was not on the agenda and could not be discussed. He then announced the adjournment of the meeting.

Shengjing Maru Uncovers Kidnapping of Young Girl 108

Last night at 9:30 PM, the Customs Water Police Station received a telephone call from Huang Yu Fu, the comprador of the Japanese Osaka Company's Nanyang-bound Shengjing Maru, reporting that a man and a woman were found in the steerage, appearing to be smuggling a young woman out of the country, and requesting that they be investigated and arrested. The police dispatched Detective Li Wenqi, along with investigator Chen Shaoting from the Women and Children Relief Association, to board the ship and bring the two individuals to the police station. According to the woman, her name is Jiang Qiaoyun, she is seventeen years old, a native of Changzhou, her father is Jiang Jintian, who is a farmer. When I was eight years old, I was adopted by my maternal uncle Zhou Dexin, a native of Wuxi, as his daughter, living at No. 1 Jiqing Lane, Dongxing Road, Wuxi. I am currently a worker in a yarn factory. A month ago, Yang Baozhu (24 years old) from Anhui opened a sesame cake shop in front of my house. He came to my house to play, and we became acquainted. He was very generous, so I stayed with him at the First Hotel for five nights, and had sexual intercourse with him more than ten times. Now I am willing to go to Fujian with him as his wife, etc. According to Yang Baozhu, he used to be the bugler of the Third Company of the Fifth Regiment of the Fujian Security Brigade. He was discharged two months ago and returned to Wuxi to open a shop. Because Qiaoyun voluntarily wanted to marry me, I accompanied her to Fujian to make a living, etc. The detective then found a short-term leave certificate issued by the regimental commander of the Fifth Regiment on Yang's person. He further questioned Yang, asking why he was opening a shop in Wuxi when he had not been discharged, obviously plotting to seduce Qiaoyun and sell her abroad. Yang lowered his head and said nothing upon hearing this. The detective further questioned Qiaoyun, asking if her parents knew that you were coming to Shanghai. Qiaoyun replied that her uncle and aunt did not know at all. The detective concluded that the case was clear. Yang Baozhu's seduction of a good family's daughter, first raping her and then selling her, was truly heinous. He ordered that they be sent to the local court for trial in the afternoon.

Lu Clan Ancestral Hall Rectifies Public Property 109

Lu Zijie et al. Lose Lawsuit for Base Land; Li Tixian et al.'s Appeal Rejected

The Lu clan ancestral hall in the Lan Ni Bo Plain in Pudong, Shanghai (i.e., the ancestral hall of the virtuous Lu Wenyu), has been diligently carrying out the work of rectifying the ancestral hall's public property since this spring, when its clansmen organized a public property rectification committee. Because Li Tixian and Lu Dao colluded with Cui to steal and sell land under the name of Lu Tushan, which was part of the public property, they sued Li Tixian et al. and won. Now, it has been discovered that more than three mu of land belonging to the Lu clan cemetery owned by the association was recently claimed by the Lu Zijie brothers, who styled themselves as direct descendants of Wenyu, hoping to make an unreasonable claim to the property. After the chairman of the association committee, Lu Zhiqing, and the lawyer he hired, Mr. Gao Junxiang, presented various pieces of evidence to prove in detail that the land had always belonged to the ancestral hall, the local court ruled the day before yesterday, confirming that the land belonged to the Lu clan ancestral hall. As for Li Xunxian et al.'s theft and sale of land under the name of Lu Tushan, after the first instance judgment ordered its return, Li Tixian et al. refused to accept it and appealed. It is said that the Suzhou High Court has also rejected their appeal.

Chinese Ancient Coin Society Holds Research Meeting Yesterday 112

The Chinese Ancient Coin Society held its seventh research meeting yesterday. More than 20 people attended, including Hu Puan, Ding Fubao, Xu Peikun, Yang Kailing, Zhang Feng, and Wei Juxian. The research topic was "Chichi Wuzhu." Mr. Zhang Jiliang elaborated in great detail. The Chichi Wuzhu was cast during the Yuanding reign of Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty and was worth ten times its face value. At that time, the people paid taxes and could not use anything other than Chichi. The Book of Han wrote "赤側 (chì cè)" as "赤仄 (chì zè)", which is because the Shuowen said that 仄 (zè) originally meant 側 (cè). In addition, the second issue of the society's journal, Ancient Coins, has been published. It contains Weng Yiquan's unedited manuscript of Ancient Coin Compilations, which is particularly valuable. In addition, there are great works by Xu Yugong, Luo Bozhao, Ding Fubao, and Shu Juxian. The content of the book is rich and includes a photocopy of a posthumous note written by Bao Zinian (Kang) in his own handwriting. It is said that it is still sold by the Medical Book Bureau, Shanghai Magazine Company, and the author's bookstore.

Ms. Niu Huizhu, wife of Guo Yangmo, sister of the famous doctors Niu Huilin and Niu Huisheng, unfortunately suffered from heart disease and suddenly passed away on the morning of the 15th.

The funeral was originally scheduled for yesterday, but it was postponed to await the return of her brother from Chengdu, who was hurrying back. The funeral was held last night, and the Christian funeral service will be held today (September 18th) at 3:00 PM, followed by the burial at the Hongqiao International Cemetery. Friends from all walks of life of the Guo and Niu families will attend to pay their respects.

University Student Convicted of Beating Cook to Death; He Cangyun Sentenced to Three Years and Six Months 118

He Cangyun, a student at St. John's University in Fanwangdu, and Li Gan, found a fly in their egg fried rice and fined the cook Zhang Yuanquan one dollar, guaranteeing to return it if they did not get sick within a week. After a week passed without incident, Zhang asked He to return the dollar. A verbal dispute ensued, and He punched Zhang in the head, resulting in his death. The police station detained He and Li and sent them to the local court for prosecution on charges of causing death by injury. After a clear trial by Judge Xie, the verdict was announced yesterday: He Cangyun was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment, and Li Gan was found not guilty.

Unified Transport and Sales of Anhui and Jiangxi Black Tea This Year Has Achieved Excellent Results; Improving International Reputation by Destroying Inferior Tea; Prices Increased and Settlement Was Expedited; Minister Wu Shi Deeply Commended This 119

The governments of Anhui and Jiangxi provinces, in order to revive the export of black tea and assist tea farmers, specially established the Anhui and Jiangxi Black Tea Sales Transport Committee and set up a Black Tea General Transport and Sales Office in Shanghai to handle sales affairs. Now that the black tea season is about to pass, the Transport and Sales Office is about to close. For the sake of assistance, the Transport and Sales Committee specially dispatched three committee members to Shanghai yesterday. The reporter of the Shenshi News Agency investigated and recorded the details as follows:

Increased Production; Tea Merchants Profited; The governments of Anhui and Jiangxi provinces, in order to assist tea farmers and revive the export of black tea, implemented unified transport and sales this spring with the assistance of the Ministry of Industry. In May, the Black Tea Transport and Sales Committee was established, and the Black Tea General Transport and Sales Office was set up in Shanghai, appointing Cheng Zhenji and Hui Zhen as general manager and deputy manager, respectively, to be responsible for sales affairs. On the one hand, they negotiated sales methods with foreign firms, and on the other hand, they raised funds of 1.8 to 1.9 million yuan to lend to tea merchants at low interest. A total of more than 100 tea merchants in Anhui and Jiangxi produced more than 72,000 boxes of Qihong tea and more than 8,000 boxes of Ning tea this year. As of the 15th of this month, more than 72,000 boxes have been sold, accounting for 90% of the total value. The tea merchants have profited more than 1 million yuan in total. Only more than 8,100 boxes remain unsold, and it is decided that they will be sold out by the end of September.

Dispatching Personnel to Shanghai to Destroy Inferior Tea

Because the black tea season is about to end, the Anhui and Jiangxi Black Tea Transport and Sales Committee intends to end this year's black tea business early. It has specially dispatched three committee members, Chen Ding, Lu Zhaomei, and He Chongjie, to Shanghai to assist the Shanghai General Transport and Sales Office in handling the closure. Three methods have been decided upon: (1) Wholesale the remaining unsold black tea; (2) Set a deadline for settling outstanding accounts; (3) Streamline the organization. Regarding the sale of remaining tea, the Tea Quality Assessment Committee of the Transport and Sales Office has now graded the tea and is contacting various tea buying foreign firms to negotiate prices. Jardine Matheson, Concord, Jinlong, Zai Yu Tai, etc., are all interested in purchasing and are competing to increase prices. The deal is expected to be finalized within a day or two. However, among the remaining tea, there are inevitably a few inferior teas. More than 100 boxes that have been inspected and found to be substandard by the Quality Assessment Committee will not be allowed to be exported. It has been decided that they will be removed and burned to avoid affecting the reputation of black tea from the two provinces. The Social Affairs Bureau and Chinese and foreign tea merchant associations will be invited to the site to supervise at that time. Specific methods have also been set for settlement and streamlining, and it is expected that they will be completely completed by the end of October.

Minister Wu Commends the Transport and Sales Results

As for the effect of the Anhui and Jiangxi Black Tea Transport and Sales Office this year, it is: (1) The price has increased. The highest value this year is 50% higher than last year; (2) The settlement has been expedited. In previous years, the settlement period had to be until the end of the year, and sometimes even as late as January or February of the following year, while this year, the sale will be completed in September and the closure in October, which is three months earlier. Other tea farmers have also benefited a lot. The above points are sufficient to show the effectiveness of unified transport and sales. Externally, due to the improved quality and perfect packaging, the reputation of tea in foreign countries has been increased. It is also known that Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industry recently came to Anhui to provide instructions on everything and deeply commended the achievements of the unified transport and sales of black tea. In order to discuss plans for next year, the Transport and Sales Committee will hold a meeting in Jiangxi in October to decide on methods.

Accused of Murder: Stage Manager of Xiang Theater Sentenced - Wang Shubao Sentenced to 13 Years Imprisonment - Zhang Xiaowanzi Convicted of Perjury 122

Wang Shubao from Yancheng, the owner of the Xiang Theater, was involved in a case during the January 28th Shanghai Incident at Hongkou Xiangyan Bridge, where a dismissed detective, Ji Zhongtang, was shot and killed. Someone distributed leaflets accusing Wang of colluding with Wang Sanshizi (Wang Thirty Son) Zheng Xiaoheizi to orchestrate this tragedy due to a dispute over the actress Yu Yanfang. The District Court Prosecutor detained Wang and indicted him along with the original accuser, Zhang Xiaowanzi. After repeated trials and debates in the criminal court, Judge Yu held a hearing yesterday and announced the verdict: Wang Shubao was found guilty of joint murder and sentenced to 13 years of imprisonment. Zhang Xiaowanzi was found guilty of perjury and sentenced to two years of imprisonment. The reasons for the verdict were explained to Wang Shubao, stating that the witnesses testified that it was not him who committed the murder, and the victim's family also stated that it was not him. However, Zhang Xiaowanzi, three days after Ji Zhongtang's death, had identified him in the presence of Ji Chenshi. Now, Zhang Xiaowanzi says it was not him, therefore the suspicion of perjury against him is established, and the case is serious, so he cannot be acquitted. However, if he does not agree, he can appeal. The judge also told the defense lawyer that if he appeals, there is favorable evidence that when Zhang Xiaowanzi reported the death of Ji Zhongtang on his behalf, he said that the murderer Wang Shushi had pockmarks and a Northern accent, so in the appeal reasons, it is appropriate to seek strong counter-evidence in this regard. Since Wang Shubao is guilty, Zhang Xiaowanzi is naturally guilty. The lawyers requested bail, and the judge instructed them to submit a written request to the court for consideration with the prosecutor, and then ordered him to be returned to custody.

Malaria Increasingly Rampant in the Public Concession Last Month - Dysentery Increased But Not Very Concerning - Cholera Can Be Said to Have Been Avoided This Year 125

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Health Department report for August states that the most noteworthy point regarding the sanitation situation in the Concession during that month was the increasing prevalence of malaria. The number of malaria cases in July increased by 64 compared to June, totaling 96 cases, and in August, it increased again to as many as 157 cases, which is a worrying phenomenon. Moreover, its source is the same as the previous month, with a large number of cases occurring in the Eastern District, and it has been determined that as many as 45 cases came from a certain location. Currently, the mobile mosquito eradication team has been spraying mosquito repellent into stagnant water in the East and West districts, and the effect is quite good. The concern is that other mosquito breeding sites are not under the jurisdiction of the Concession, and there is a possibility of sporadic outbreaks at any time. Furthermore, although mosquito eradication is the key to preventing malaria, the prevention efforts of private residences should not be ignored. Setting up screens in the homes of wealthy families is an essential measure, and spraying with petroleum-based insecticide should also be carried out daily without interruption. Regarding the matter of screens, although the price of copper wire screens is slightly higher, they are durable and more cost-effective than other inferior products. In addition, the window frames should be made of dry wood to prevent them from bending and forming gaps after they are made, allowing mosquitoes to enter the room.

Dysentery also increased in August, but this is due to the season and is not a cause for great concern. Other gastrointestinal diseases are not significantly different from last year. Furthermore, this year's fly eradication work has been very effective, but the hot weather is also unfavorable for the reproduction of flies, and it is feared that flies will breed again after the weather cools down in the autumn, so it is hoped that citizens will pay more attention to assistance, and unclean objects should not be dumped everywhere, but should be placed in garbage cans and covered. Fly traps should also be prepared in large quantities.

Furthermore, many cases of rabies were discovered in August, which is very concerning. The reason is that stray dogs from outside the Concession have entered the Concession. Regarding the issue of cholera, 38 patients were tested in August, but no true cholera bacteria were found. Now that the weather has cooled down, a major outbreak can be avoided this year.

Unexpectedly, at around 9:00 PM the night before, Chen Caizhen saw Wang Boquan also arrive while working at the New World, so she called Chinese police officer number 2684 and arrested Wang. The original stolen pocket watch was found on his person and taken to the Xinzha Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to Criminal Court Eight of the First Special Court. Lawyer Zhang Tianyin from the Police Station described the case, saying that the Wuxi Public Security Bureau was not yet aware of the case, so he requested permission to detain Wang in order to notify the Wuxi Public Security Bureau to send someone to pick him up. Chen Caizhen and Zhou Yindi also confessed the above situation. Wang Boquan was questioned and gave evasive answers. Judge Chuan ordered Wang to be detained and rescheduled the hearing, pending notification to the Wuxi Public Security Bureau to send someone to court for verification.

Inside the criminal holding room behind the First Tribunal of the Second Special District Court, at around 2:00 PM on the 15th, two thieves, Wu Asan and Wang Agen, escaped by prying open the iron fence on the back door. Wang had a lighter responsibility and was ordered to be dismissed and await review. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. According to Xiao Along, he is 41 years old, from Yancheng, and lives in a bungalow in Yonghe Lane, Haining Road. He used to do a sock factory business, but recently became unemployed. He was arrested for stealing a wallet and was taken to the waiting room at around 10:00 AM on the 15th, along with nine other people. The police officer did not take the key to the back door, and after a while, five people were taken away before the key was taken away. At around 2:00 PM in the afternoon, it was discovered that two people had gone down from the back door and did not return, so it was assumed that they had escaped, so the police officer was immediately notified. The two escapees took off their clothes outside the back door and left behind two hats, etc. Gu Wanrong confessed that he was 17 years old, from Ningbo, and lived in Tilanqiao making light bulbs. He was arrested for theft. He was taken to the waiting room at around 10:00 AM on the 15th. The other two (referring to the escapees) were looking out the window before they escaped. One person said, "There is a foreigner here, it's okay." Later, I fell asleep. It was Xiao who discovered that they had escaped and then knew that the two had actually escaped. Zhang Munniu's confession was the same as Gu's. Finally, police officers No. 515 and No. 141 were questioned. According to No. 515, although I was in charge of the key, it was hung on the window outside the front door of the waiting room, and any police officer could take the key to open the door. This has always been the case. No. 141 said that when No. 515 returned from lunch, I handed over the prisoners to him, and no one was missing. I don't know how they escaped. After verifying the confessions, the court ordered Xiao Gu and Zhang, the three inmates, to be returned to the police station for detention. The two police officers were ordered to be dismissed and await review. In the afternoon, after Prosecutor Wang investigated, he considered that police officer No. 515 Jiang Fengyuan was more responsible and issued an order not to allow bail, and ordered him to be detained in the detention center to await prosecution.

Lu Yuanhu's Funeral Held Yesterday 136

Lu Pei, the chief of the Hengfeng Road Police Station, was sued in the District Court by representatives Peng Yuanfeng, Liao Benxiang, Liu Zhaocai, and others representing thousands of poor people from hundreds of straw sheds on Changan Road, Zhabei, for abusing his power, forcibly demolishing straw sheds, and causing harm to the people, causing thousands of poor people to fall into despair. After repeated trials, yesterday was the final debate hearing. The plaintiffs said that the defendant abused his power to forcibly demolish straw sheds without the order of the Public Security Bureau and the request of the owner Gu Lanzhou, obstructing the freedom of the people, and should be prosecuted according to law. Lu Pei argued that he was acting on the instructions of his superiors. Each gave eloquent arguments on the evidence for a long time. The judge announced the end of the debate and scheduled the sentencing for the 23rd.

Zhou Bangjun, General Manager of Zhongxi Pharmacy, Donates the Qiu Feihai Memorial Cup 149

The trophy is named "Mingxing Cup", entrusted to the Physical Education Association for safekeeping and planning. The donated funds have been remitted to the family members, and continued donations are encouraged.

Since the start of fundraising for the late tennis player Qiu Feihai Memorial Cup, there have been very few donors. It was immediately notified to the initiator, Mr. Hu Xiansheng.

Hu Xiansheng Talks

According to Mr. Hu, the memorial cup competition has been contacted with the Sports Promotion Association and is planning everything. Generally, a committee will be formed by the Association to keep it in custody. Mr. Zhou's righteous act is very rare. In addition to preparing a letter of thanks, the donations received have been remitted to Mr. Qiu's family as instructed. However, Qiu's mother and wife are still in a foreign land, looking at the motherland from afar, and they are suffering from a lack of funds for living. Even if the Cup revenue were water from a cart, it would be difficult to reverse the course. I hope that all sectors will have pity and continue to contribute donations so that Mr. Qiu's mother and wife can avoid drifting in a foreign land. The original letter from Mr. Zhou is recorded as follows:

Mr. Zhou's Original Letter

Dear Sir, I recently read in the newspaper that your bank is collecting donations for Mr. Qiu Feihai's memorial cup. Although there are donors, the donations are not enthusiastic. A generation of national tennis players, their souls are difficult to comfort underground. Our company attaches great importance to sports and admires Mr. Qiu's life very much. Unfortunately, he died of illness in a foreign land, and we deeply mourn him. We are now willing to contribute 500 yuan from the surplus of the Mingxing Perfume produced by our company, and entrust the Standard Sports Equipment Company to design and manufacture a Mingxing Cup, specially engraved with words commemorating Mr. Qiu. As for the competition management method, it is proposed that the National Sports Promotion Association organize a committee to plan it. We hope that your bank will convey this intention to Mr. Hu Xiansheng, the initiator of the Qiu Jun Memorial Cup. As for the memorial cup donations that have been received at this time, it is not necessary to directly remit them to the Qiu family. I send this letter to the Qiu Feihai Memorial Cup Collection Office of Xinhua Bank, Zhou Bangjun, General Manager of Zhongxi Pharmacy, September 16.

The news that world professional tennis stars Teirden van Ness and Miss Shabod were coming to Shanghai was once rumored. The date of arrival in Shanghai is November 2nd or 5th, because there are two ships to Shanghai at this time, the former is a US postal ship, which arrives in Shanghai at about 10:00 AM and must leave the port at 6:00 PM in the afternoon. During this urgent period, if it unfortunately rains, it may be difficult to attend the performance. The latter is a French ship, which has a three-day stay, which is more abundant. The scheduled number of performances has been declared to be still under consideration. Recently, the Linshan Conference has been very prosperous again, and Tie and others have also stayed there, so they have not been able to decide for a long time. As for the number of performances in Shanghai, Mr. Ka said that he thought that he would have to wait until Tie and others arrived in Japan before making a definitive statement.
